        the registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule&#160;405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405 of this

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Shareholders also (1)&nbsp;approved named executive officer compensation,
(2)&nbsp;approved an annual vote on Associated Banc-Corp&rsquo;s named executive officer compensation, and (3)&nbsp;ratified the selection
of KPMG LLP as Associated&rsquo;s independent accounting firm for 2024.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B><U>Dividends Declared</U></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">The Associated Board of Directors declared a regular quarterly cash
dividend of $0.22 per common share, payable on June&nbsp;17, 2024, to shareholders of record at the close of business on June&nbsp;3,
2024.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">The Board of Directors also declared a regular quarterly cash dividend
of $0.3671875 per depositary share on Associated&rsquo;s 5.875% Series&nbsp;E Perpetual Preferred Stock, payable on June&nbsp;17, 2024,
to shareholders of record at the close of business on June&nbsp;3, 2024.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">The Board of Directors also declared a regular quarterly cash dividend
of $0.3515625 per depositary share on Associated&rsquo;s 5.625% Series&nbsp;F Perpetual Preferred Stock, payable on June&nbsp;17, 2024,
to shareholders of record at the close of business on June&nbsp;3, 2024.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>ABOUT ASSOCIATED BANC-CORP</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Associated Banc-Corp (NYSE: ASB) has total assets
of $41 billion and is the largest bank holding company based in Wisconsin. Headquartered in Green Bay, Wisconsin, Associated is a leading
Midwest banking franchise, offering a full range of financial products and services from nearly 200 banking locations serving more than
100 communities throughout Wisconsin,&nbsp;Illinois and Minnesota. The Company also operates loan production offices in Indiana, Michigan,
Missouri, New York, Ohio and Texas. Associated Bank, N.A. is an Equal Housing Lender, Equal Opportunity Lender and Member FDIC. More information
about Associated Banc-Corp is available at www.associatedbank.com.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>
